>> /*
>> * Constrains containers to a desired aspect ratio
>> * See https://css-tricks.com/snippets/sass/maintain-aspect-ratio-mixin/
>> */
>> /**
>>  * Assigns z-index values from top to bottom in correspondence
>>  * with the order of the the selector list.
>>  *
>>  * Examples:
>>  *
>>  * Given @selctors: '.top', '.middle', '.bottom';
>>  * .mapZIndices(@selectors); would render as
>>  * .top {
>>  *   z-index: 1000;
>>  * }
>>  * .middle {
>>  *   z-index: 990;
>>  * }
>>  * .bottom {
>>  *   z-index: 980;
>>  * }
>>  *
>>  * .mapZIndices(@selectors; 1200; 50); would render as
>>  * .top {
>>  *   z-index: 1200;
>>  * }
>>  * .middle {
>>  *   z-index: 1150;
>>  * }
>>  * .bottom {
>>  *   z-index: 1100;
>>  * }
>>  *
>>  * @param {List[String]} selectorList
>>  *                         list of selector strings
>>  * @param {Number}       ceiling
>>  *                         highest z-index value assigned
>>  * @param {Number}       step
>>  *                         gap between consecutively assigned z-indices
>>  */
>> .z3d-attribution {
>>   position: absolute;
>>   left: 0;
>>   top: 0;
>>   display: inline-flex;
>>   align-items: center;
>>   margin: 16px 0 0 8px;
>>   font-size: 0.8em;
>>   text-shadow: 0 2px 3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.65);
>>   color: #FFF;
>>   opacity: 0;
>>   z-index: 10000;
>>   -webkit-user-select: none;
>>   -moz-user-select: none;
>>   -o-user-select: none;
>>   -ms-user-select: none;
>>   user-select: none;
>>   -webkit-transition: opacity 0.15s ease-out 3s;
>>   -moz-transition: opacity 0.15s ease-out 3s;
>>   -ms-transition: opacity 0.15s ease-out 3s;
>>   -o-transition: opacity 0.15s ease-out 3s;
>>   transition: opacity 0.15s ease-out 3s;
>> }

>>   }

>> /*
>> * Constrains containers to a desired aspect ratio
>> * See https://css-tricks.com/snippets/sass/maintain-aspect-ratio-mixin/
>> */
>> /**
>>  * Assigns z-index values from top to bottom in correspondence
>>  * with the order of the the selector list.
>>  *
>>  * Examples:
>>  *
>>  * Given @selctors: '.top', '.middle', '.bottom';
>>  * .mapZIndices(@selectors); would render as
>>  * .top {
>>  *   z-index: 1000;
>>  * }
>>  * .middle {
>>  *   z-index: 990;
>>  * }
>>  * .bottom {
>>  *   z-index: 980;
>>  * }
>>  *
>>  * .mapZIndices(@selectors; 1200; 50); would render as
>>  * .top {
>>  *   z-index: 1200;
>>  * }
>>  * .middle {
>>  *   z-index: 1150;
>>  * }
>>  * .bottom {
>>  *   z-index: 1100;
>>  * }
>>  *
>>  * @param {List[String]} selectorList
>>  *                         list of selector strings
>>  * @param {Number}       ceiling
>>  *                         highest z-index value assigned
>>  * @param {Number}       step
>>  *                         gap between consecutively assigned z-indices
>>  */
